| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|

| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka ACL Authorization Code Audit

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in `apache/kafka` that implement or define Access Control List (ACL) authorization logic. Search under `core/src/main/` and `clients/src/main/` for files containing classes or interfaces with `Authorizer` or `AclAuthorizer` in the name. For each file, report the class name and whether it defines the interface, implements it, or provides test utilities.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

Done! I've completed the Kafka ACL authorization code audit. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I discovered **21 key Java files** related to ACL authorization logic in the Apache Kafka codebase:

### Core Components

**Main Interfaces (clients/src/main/):**
- **Authorizer.java** - The primary pluggable interface for authorization with methods for authorization checks, ACL management, and startup
- **AuthorizerServerInfo.java** - Interface providing broker metadata to authorizers
- **AuthorizableRequestContext.java** - Interface providing request context to authorization logic

**Extended Interface:**
- **ClusterMetadataAuthorizer.java** - Extension for KRaft-based authorizers that store ACLs in cluster metadata

**Built-in Implementation:**
- **StandardAuthorizer.java** - The modern, concrete implementation storing ACLs in the __cluster_metadata log (implements ClusterMetadataAuthorizer and Monitorable)
- **KafkaAuthorizerServerInfo.java** - Concrete implementation of AuthorizerServerInfo

### Supporting Infrastructure

**Authorization Models:**
- Action.java, AuthorizationResult.java (enum: ALLOWED/DENIED)
- AclCreateResult.java, AclDeleteResult.java

**Metadata/Data Management:**
- StandardAcl.java, StandardAuthorizerData.java, AclCache.java
- AclMutator.java, StandardAclRecordIterator.java, StandardAclWithId.java
- AclPublisher.java (handles ACL updates from metadata)

**Utilities:**
- AuthorizerUtils.java (factory for creating authorizers with metrics)
- AclEntry.java (ACL constants and helper methods)
- AuthorizerNotReadyException.java

**Test Utilities:**
- MonitorableAuthorizer (test implementation in AuthorizerUtilsTest.java)

For each connection, broker performs authentication and then accepts Kafka requests.\n56:  *       For each request, broker invokes {@link #authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List)} to authorize\n57:  *       actions performed by the request.</li>\n58:  * </ol>\n59:  *\n60:  * Authorizer implementation class may optionally implement @{@link org.apache.kafka.common.Reconfigurable}\n61:  * to enable dynamic reconfiguration without restarting the broker.\n62:  * <p>Authorizer implementation class may also optionally implement {@link org.apache.kafka.common.metrics.Monitorable}\n63:  * to enable the authorizer to register metrics. The following tags are automatically added to all metrics registered:\n64:  * <code>config</code> set to <code>authorizer.class.name</code>, <code>class</code> set to the Authorizer class name,\n65:  * and <code>role</code> set to either <code>broker</code> or <code>controller</code>.\n66:  * <p>\n67:  * <b>Threading model:</b>\n68:  * <ul>\n69:  *   <li>All authorizer operations including authorization and ACL updates must be thread-safe.</li>\n70:  *   <li>ACL update methods are asynchronous. Implementations with low update latency may return a\n71:  *       completed future using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}.\n72:  *       This ensures that the request will be handled synchronously by the caller without using a\n73:  *       purgatory to wait for the result. If ACL updates require remote communication which may block,\n74:  *       return a future that is completed asynchronously when the remote operation completes. This enables\n75:  *       the caller to process other requests on the request threads without blocking.</li>\n76:  *   <li>Any threads or thread pools used for processing remote operations asynchronously can be started during\n77:  *       {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}. These threads must be shutdown during {@link Authorizer#close()}.</li>\n78:  * </ul>\n79:  * </p>\n80:  */\n81: public interface Authorizer extends Configurable, Closeable {\n82: \n83:     /**\n84:      * Starts loading authorization metadata and returns futures that can be used to wait until\n85:      * metadata for authorizing requests on each listener is available. ACL Authorization Code Audit\\n\\n### Summary\\nFound comprehensive ACL authorization implementation in Apache Kafka spanning across core, clients, metadata, and server modules. The authorization architecture includes the main Authorizer interface, a ClusterMetadataAuthorizer extension, the StandardAuthorizer implementation, and supporting infrastructure for ACL management.\\n\\n### Core Architecture\\n\\n**Main Interface Definition:**\\n- **Authorizer.java** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/authorizer/): Defines the pluggable authorizer interface for Kafka brokers. This is the primary interface that all authorizer implementations must implement. It includes methods for:\\n  - start(AuthorizerServerInfo): Initialize the authorizer\\n  - authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List<Action>): Perform authorization checks\\n  - createAcls/deleteAcls: Manage ACL bindings\\n  - acls(AclBindingFilter): Query ACL bindings\\n  - authorizeByResourceType: Default method for checking authorization by resource type\\n\\n**Extended Interface:**\\n- **ClusterMetadataAuthorizer.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/): Extends Authorizer for authorizers that store state in the __cluster_metadata log. Includes additional methods:\\n  - setAclMutator/aclMutatorOrException: Manage the ACL mutator\\n  - completeInitialLoad: Signal completion of initial load\\n  - loadSnapshot: Load ACLs from snapshot\\n  - addAcl/removeAcl: Manage ACLs directly\\n\\n**Built-in Implementation:**\\n- **StandardAuthorizer.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/): Concrete implementation of ClusterMetadataAuthorizer. This is the modern, built-in authorizer that stores ACLs in the cluster metadata log. Implements the Monitorable interface for metrics support.\\n\\n**Server Info Implementation:**\\n- **KafkaAuthorizerServerInfo.java** (server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/network/): Concrete implementation of AuthorizerServerInfo interface providing runtime broker configuration metadata to authorizers during startup.\\n\\n### Supporting Interfaces\\n\\n**Request Context & Metadata:**\\n- **AuthorizerServerInfo.java** (clients/src/main/java): Interface for runtime broker configuration metadata including cluster resource, broker ID, endpoints, inter-broker endpoint, and early start listeners.\\n- **AuthorizableRequestContext.java** (clients/src/main/java): Interface providing request context data including listener name, security protocol, principal, client address, request type/version/ID, and correlation ID.\\n\\n**Authorization Models:**\\n- **Action.java** (clients/src/main/java): Class representing an action being authorized with resource pattern, operation, reference count, and logging flags.\\n- **AuthorizationResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Enum with ALLOWED and DENIED states for authorization decisions.\\n\\n**Result Classes:**\\n- **AclCreateResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Result class for ACL creation operations with optional exception.\\n- **AclDeleteResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Result class for ACL deletion operations with exception and binding delete results.\\n\\n### Metadata and Data Management\\n\\n**ACL Storage Interfaces:**\\n- **AclMutator.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Interface implemented by QuorumController for ACL create and delete operations in ClusterMetadataAuthorizer instances.\\n\\n**Data Classes:**\\n- **StandardAcl.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Represents a Kafka ACL identified by UUID and stored in metadata log.\\n- **StandardAuthorizerData.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Immutable class holding ACL data for KRaft-based clusters.\\n- **AclCache.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Immutable cache storing ACLs sorted by resource and indexed by UUID.\\n- **StandardAclRecordIterator.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Iterator for batch retrieval of ACL records.\\n- **StandardAclWithId.java** (metadata/src/main/java): ACL representation with associated UUID.\\n\\n**ACL Publisher:**\\n- **AclPublisher.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/publisher/): Handles ACL updates from metadata snapshots and incremental changes, notifying ClusterMetadataAuthorizer instances.\\n\\n### Utility Classes\\n\\n**Authorization Utilities:**\\n- **AuthorizerUtils.java** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/): Utility class for creating and wrapping authorizer instances with metrics. Contains createAuthorizer() method.\\n- **AclEntry.java** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/): Utility class providing ACL constants and helper methods including:\\n  - Wildcard definitions for principals and hosts\\n  - supportedOperations(ResourceType): Returns valid operations per resource type\\n  - authorizationError(ResourceType): Maps resource types to error codes\\n\\n**Exception:**\\n- **AuthorizerNotReadyException.java** (clients/src/main/java): RetriableException indicating the authorizer is not yet ready to process requests.\\n\\n### Test Utilities\\n\\n**Test Implementation:**\\n- **MonitorableAuthorizer** (in AuthorizerUtilsTest.java, server/src/test/java): Test utility implementing Authorizer and Monitorable for testing metrics integration. Broker creates authorizer instance from configured class name (AuthorizerUtils.createAuthorizer)\\n2. Broker calls authorizer.start() with server metadata\\n3. For KRaft-based clusters, StandardAuthorizer loads initial ACLs from metadata snapshot\\n4. ACLPublisher updates authorizer as ACLs change in cluster metadata\\n5. For each request, broker calls authorize() with action list\\n6. StandardAuthorizer consults cached ACLs to make authorization decisions\\n7. ACL mutations go through AclMutator interface to QuorumController\\n\\nAll code is located in the github.com/sg-evals/kafka--0753c489 repository across multiple modules.\"\n}\n",
